================



 Posted in **MTGO Standings**
 on June 19, 2022

* [Decklists](#decklists)
* [Standings](#standings)

Bracket
-------





### Quarterfinals






**(1) Brivenix, 2-1**

**(4) LuckyOnline, 2-1**






 (5) unicornparadise

 (4) LuckyOnline

### Finals






**(1) Brivenix, 2-0**






 (2) Kirblinxy
